string.\n   215→\n   216→        Produces a machine-readable YAML document with standardized fields\n   217→        for downstream tooling and TUI display.\n   218→        \"\"\"\n   219→        lines = [\n   220→            f\"phase: {self.phase_number}\",\n   221→            f\"status: {self.status}\",\n   222→            f\"tasks_total: {self.tasks_total}\",\n   223→            f\"tasks_passed: {self.tasks_passed}\",\n   224→            f\"tasks_failed: {self.tasks_failed}\",\n   225→            f\"tasks_incomplete: {self.tasks_incomplete}\",\n   226→            f\"tasks_not_attempted: {self.tasks_not_attempted}\",\n   227→            f\"budget_remaining: {self.budget_remaining}\",\n   228→            f\"total_turns_consumed: {self.total_turns_consumed}\",\n   229→            f\"total_duration_seconds: {self.total_duration_seconds:.1f}\",\n   230→            \"tasks:\",\n   231→        ]\n   232→        for tr in self.task_results:\n   233→            lines.append(f\"  - task_id: {tr.task.task_id}\")\n   234→            lines.append(f\"    title: \\\"{tr.task.title}\\\"\")\n   235→            lines.append(f\"    status: {tr.status.value}\")\n   236→            lines.append(f\"    gate_outcome: {tr.gate_outcome.value}\")\n   237→            lines.append(f\"    turns_consumed: {tr.turns_consumed}\")\n   238→            lines.append(f\"    duration_seconds: {tr.duration_seconds:.1f}\")\n   239→        if self.remaining_task_ids:\n   240→            lines.append(\"remaining_tasks:\")\n   241→            for tid in self.remaining_task_ids:\n   242→                lines.append(f\"  - {tid}\")\n   243→        return \"\\n\".join(lines) + \"\\n\"\n   244→\n   245→    def to_markdown(self) -> str:\n   246→        \"\"\"Render the report as a markdown string with YAML frontmatter.\"\"\"\n   247→        lines = [\n   248→            \"---\",\n   249→            f\"phase: {self.phase_number}\",\n   250→            f\"status: {self.status}\",\n   251→            f\"tasks_total: {self.tasks_total}\",\n   252→            f\"tasks_passed: {self.tasks_passed}\",\n   253→            f\"tasks_failed: {self.tasks_failed}\",\n   254→            \"---\",\n   255→            \"\",\n   256→            f\"# Phase {self.phase_number} — Aggregated Task Report\",\n   257→            \"\",\n   258→            \"| Task ID | Title | Status | Turns | Duration |\",\n   259→            \"|---------|-------|--------|-------|----------|\",\n   260→        ]\n   261→        for tr in self.task_results:\n   262→            dur = f\"{tr.duration_seconds:.1f}s\"\n   263→            lines.append(\n   264→                f\"| {tr.task.task_id} | {tr.task.title} | {tr.status.value} \"\n   265→                f\"| {tr.turns_consumed} | {dur} |\"\n   266→            )\n   267→        lines.append(\"\")\n   268→        lines.append(f\"**Total turns consumed:** {self.total_turns_consumed}\")\n   269→        lines.append(f\"**Total duration:** {self.total_duration_seconds:.1f}s\")\n   270→\n   271→        if self.remaining_task_ids:\n   272→            lines.append(\"\")\n   273→            lines.append(\"## Remaining Tasks (Budget Exhausted)\")\n   274→            for tid in self.remaining_task_ids:\n   275→                lines.append(f\"- {tid}\")\n   276→\n   277→        lines.append(\"\")\n   278→        if self.status == \"PASS\":\n   279→            lines.append(\"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\")\n   280→        else:\n   281→            lines.append(\"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT\")\n   282→\n   283→        return \"\\n\".join(lines) + \"\\n\"\n   284→\n   285→\n   286→def aggregate_task_results(\n   287→    phase_number: int,\n   288→    task_results: list[TaskResult],\n   289→    remaining_task_ids: list[str] | None = None,\n   290→    budget_remaining: int = 0,\n   291→) -> AggregatedPhaseReport:\n   292→    \"\"\"Aggregate individual TaskResults into a runner-constructed PhaseReport.\n   293→\n   294→    This function is the runner's authoritative source of task outcomes.\n   295→    It does not rely on agent self-reporting.\n   296→\n   297→    Args:\n   298→        phase_number: The phase number being aggregated.\n   299→        task_results: List of TaskResult from execute_phase_tasks().\n   300→        remaining_task_ids: Task IDs that were not attempted due to budget.\n   301→\n   302→    Returns:\n   303→        AggregatedPhaseReport with computed counts and status.\n   304→    \"\"\"\n   305→    report = AggregatedPhaseReport(\n   306→        phase_number=phase_number,\n   307→        task_results=task_results,\n   308→        remaining_task_ids=remaining_task_ids or [],\n   309→        budget_remaining=budget_remaining,\n   310→    )\n   311→\n   312→    report.tasks_total = len(task_results) + len(report.remaining_task_ids)\n   313→    report.tasks_passed = sum(\n   314→        1 for r in task_results if r.status == TaskStatus.PASS\n   315→    )\n   316→    report.tasks_failed = sum(\n   317→        1 for r in task_results if r.status == TaskStatus.FAIL\n   318→    )\n   319→    report.tasks_incomplete = sum(\n   320→        1 for r in task_results if r.status == TaskStatus.INCOMPLETE\n   321→    )\n   322→    report.tasks_skipped = sum(\n   323→        1 for r in task_results if r.status == TaskStatus.SKIPPED\n   324→    )\n   325→    report.tasks_not_attempted = len(report.remaining_task_ids)\n   326→    report.total_turns_consumed = sum(r.turns_consumed for r in task_results)\n   327→    report.total_duration_seconds = sum(\n   328→        r.duration_seconds for r in task_results\n   329→    )\n   330→\n   331→    return report\n   332→\n   333→\n   334→def check_budget_guard(ledger: TurnLedger | None) -> str | None:\n   335→    \"\"\"Pre-launch budget guard: returns a halt message if budget is insufficient.\n   336→\n   337→    Returns None if launch is allowed, or a descriptive message string\n   338→    if the budget is too low to launch a subprocess.\n   339→    \"\"\"\n   340→    if ledger is None:\n   341→        return None\n   342→    if ledger.can_launch():\n   343→        return None\n   344→    return (\n   345→        f\"Budget exhausted: {ledger.available()} turns remaining, \"\n   346→        f\"minimum {ledger.minimum_allocation} required for launch\"\n   347→    )\n   348→\n   349→\n   350→def execute_phase_tasks(\n   351→    tasks: list[TaskEntry],\n   352→    config: SprintConfig,\n   353→    phase,\n   354→    ledger: TurnLedger | None = None,\n   355→    *,\n   356→    _subprocess_factory=None,\n   357→) -> tuple[list[TaskResult], list[str]]:\n   358→    \"\"\"Per-task subprocess orchestration loop.\n   359→\n   360→    Iterates over a task inventory, spawning one subprocess per task with\n   361→    budget allocation from the TurnLedger. Returns task results and a list\n   362→    of remaining (unattempted) task IDs if budget was exhausted.\n   363→\n   364→    Args:\n   365→        tasks: Ordered list of TaskEntry from the tasklist parser.\n   366→        config: Sprint configuration.\n   367→        phase: The Phase being executed.\n   368→        ledger: Optional TurnLedger for budget tracking.\n   369→        _subprocess_factory: Optional callable for testing; signature\n   370→            ``(task, config, phase) -> (exit_code, turns_consumed, output_bytes)``.\n   371→\n   372→    Returns:\n   373→        Tuple of (results, remaining_task_ids). remaining_task_ids is non-empty\n   374→        only when the loop halted due to budget exhaustion.\n   375→    \"\"\"\n   376→    results: list[TaskResult] = []\n   377→    remaining: list[str] = []\n   378→\n   379→    if not tasks:\n   380→        return results, remaining\n   381→\n   382→    for i, task in enumerate(tasks):\n   383→        started_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n   384→\n   385→        # Budget check: can we launch?\n   386→        if ledger is not None and not ledger.can_launch():\n   387→            # Mark this and all subsequent tasks as skipped\n   388→            remaining = [t.task_id for t in tasks[i:]]\n   389→            for t in tasks[i:]:\n   390→                results.append(\n   391→                    TaskResult(\n   392→                        task=t,\n   393→                        status=TaskStatus.SKIPPED,\n   394→                        started_at=started_at,\n   395→                        finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n   396→                    )\n   397→                )\n   398→            break\n   399→\n   400→        # Debit the minimum allocation upfront\n   401→        if ledger is not None:\n   402→            ledger.debit(ledger.minimum_allocation)\n   403→\n   404→        # Spawn subprocess for this task\n   405→        if _subprocess_factory is not None:\n   406→            exit_code, turns_consumed, output_bytes = _subprocess_factory(\n   407→                task, config, phase\n   408→            )\n   409→        else:\n   410→            # Default: delegate to ClaudeProcess (real execution)\n   411→            exit_code, turns_consumed, output_bytes = _run_task_subprocess(\n   412→                task, config, phase\n   413→            )\n   414→\n   415→        finished_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n   416→\n   417→        # Determine task status from exit code\n   418→        if exit_code == 0:\n   419→            status = TaskStatus.PASS\n   420→        elif exit_code == 124:\n   421→            status = TaskStatus.INCOMPLETE\n   422→        else:\n   423→            status = TaskStatus.FAIL\n   424→\n   425→        # Reconcile budget: debit actual consumption, credit back pre-allocation\n   426→        if ledger is not None:\n   427→            # We pre-debited minimum_allocation; now adjust for actual turns\n   428→            actual = max(turns_consumed, 0)\n   429→            pre_allocated = ledger.minimum_allocation\n   430→            if actual > pre_allocated:\n   431→                ledger.debit(actual - pre_allocated)\n   432→            elif actual < pre_allocated:\n   433→                ledger.credit(pre_allocated - actual)\n   434→\n   435→        results.append(\n   436→            TaskResult(\n   437→                task=task,\n   438→                status=status,\n   439→                turns_consumed=turns_consumed,\n   440→                exit_code=exit_code,\n   441→                started_at=started_at,\n   442→                finished_at=finished_at,\n   443→                output_bytes=output_bytes,\n   444→            )\n   445→        )\n   446→\n   447→    return results, remaining\n   448→\n   449→\n   450→def _run_task_subprocess(\n   451→    task: TaskEntry,\n   452→    config: SprintConfig,\n   453→    phase,\n   454→) -> tuple[int, int, int]:\n   455→    \"\"\"Run a single task in a subprocess. Returns (exit_code, turns, output_bytes).\n   456→\n   457→    This is the real implementation that spawns a ClaudeProcess. For testing,\n   458→    callers of execute_phase_tasks pass _subprocess_factory instead.\n   459→    \"\"\"\n   460→    # Build a task-specific prompt\n   461→    prompt = (\n   462→        f\"Execute task {task.task_id}: {task.title}\\n\"\n   463→        f\"From phase file: {phase.file}\\n\"\n   464→        f\"Description: {task.description}\\n\"\n   465→    )\n   466→\n   467→    proc = ClaudeProcess.__new__(ClaudeProcess)\n   468→    proc.config = config\n   469→    proc.phase = phase\n   470→    from superclaude.cli.pipeline.process import ClaudeProcess as _Base\n   471→    _Base.__init__(\n   472→        proc,\n   473→        prompt=prompt,\n   474→        output_file=config.output_file(phase),\n   475→        error_file=config.error_file(phase),\n   476→        max_turns=config.max_turns,\n   477→        model=config.model,\n   478→        permission_flag=config.permission_flag,\n   479→        timeout_seconds=config.max_turns * 120 + 300,\n   480→        output_format=\"stream-json\",\n   481→    )\n   482→    proc.start()\n   483→    proc.wait()\n   484→    exit_code = proc._process.returncode if proc._process else -1\n   485→    output_path = config.output_file(phase)\n   486→    output_bytes = output_path.stat().st_size if output_path.exists() else 0\n   487→    # Turn counting is wired separately in T02.06\n   488→    return (exit_code if exit_code is not None else -1, 0, output_bytes)\n   489→\n   490→\n   491→def execute_sprint(config: SprintConfig):\n   492→    \"\"\"Main orchestration loop.\n   493→\n   494→    For each active phase:\n   495→    1. Launch claude -p subprocess\n   496→    2. Start output monitor thread\n   497→    3. Update TUI in a polling loop until process exits (with timeout)\n   498→    4. Parse result file for CONTINUE/HALT\n   499→    5. Record PhaseResult\n   500→    6. Decide whether to continue or halt\n   501→    \"\"\"\n   502→    # Pre-flight: verify claude binary is available before starting TUI/logging\n   503→    if shutil.which(\"claude\") is None:\n   504→        raise SystemExit(\n   505→            \"Error: 'claude' binary not found in PATH. \"\n   506→            \"Install Claude Code CLI before running sprint.\"\n   507→        )\n   508→\n   509→    signal_handler = SignalHandler()\n   510→    signal_handler.install()\n   511→\n   512→    setup_debug_logger(config)\n   513→    import logging as _logging\n   514→    _dbg = _logging.getLogger(_DBG_NAME)\n   515→\n   516→    logger = SprintLogger(config)\n   517→    tui = SprintTUI(config)\n   518→    monitor = OutputMonitor(Path(\"/dev/null\"))  # reset per phase\n   519→    proc_manager: ClaudeProcess | None = None\n   520→\n   521→    sprint_result = SprintResult(config=config)\n   522→    logger.write_header(sprint_result)\n   523→\n   524→    tui.start()\n   525→\n   526→    # Startup orphan cleanup: remove stale isolation dirs from crashed previous runs\n   527→    shutil.rmtree(config.results_dir / \".isolation\", ignore_errors=True)\n   528→\n   529→    try:\n   530→        for phase in config.active_phases:\n   531→            if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n   532→                sprint_result.outcome = SprintOutcome.INTERRUPTED\n   533→                break\n   534→\n   535→            # Per-phase isolation directory: exactly one file (the phase file)\n   536→            isolation_dir = config.results_dir / \".isolation\" / f\"phase-{phase.number}\"\n   537→            isolation_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n   538→            shutil.copy2(phase.file, isolation_dir / phase.file.name)\n   539→\n   540→            try:\n   541→                # Reset monitor for this phase\n   542→                output_path = config.output_file(phase)\n   543→                monitor.reset(output_path)\n   544→                monitor.start()\n   545→\n   546→                # Update tmux tail pane if running in tmux\n   547→                if config.tmux_session_name:\n   548→                    update_tail_pane(config.tmux_session_name, output_path)\n   549→\n   550→                # Launch claude with isolation env vars (CLAUDE_WORK_DIR → isolation_dir)\n   551→                _phase_env_vars = {\n   552→                    \"CLAUDE_WORK_DIR\": str(isolation_dir),\n   553→                }\n   554→                proc_manager = ClaudeProcess(config, phase, env_vars=_phase_env_vars)\n   555→                proc_manager.start()\n   556→                started_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n   557→                # Use monotonic clock for deadline enforcement to be immune to NTP adjustments\n   558→                deadline = time.monotonic() + proc_manager.timeout_seconds\n   559→                logger.write_phase_start(phase, started_at)\n   560→\n   561→                debug_log(_dbg, \"PHASE_BEGIN\", phase=phase.number, file=str(phase.file))\n   562→\n   563→                tui.update(sprint_result, monitor.state, phase)\n   564→\n   565→                # Poll loop: wait for process to finish while updating TUI\n   566→                # Enforces monotonic timeout via deadline check.\n   567→                _timed_out = False\n   568→                _stall_acted = False  # single-fire guard for watchdog\n   569→                _poll_start = time.monotonic()\n   570→                while proc_manager._process.poll() is None:\n   571→                    if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n   572→                        proc_manager.terminate()\n   573→                        break\n   574→                    if time.monotonic() > deadline:\n   575→                        # Timeout reached: kill the process, exit loop\n   576→                        _timed_out = True\n   577→                        proc_manager.terminate()\n   578→                        break\n   579→\n   580→                    ms = monitor.state\n   581→                    _elapsed = time.monotonic() - _poll_start\n   582→\n   583→                    debug_log(\n   584→                        _dbg,\n   585→                        \"poll_tick\",\n   586→                        phase=phase.number,\n   587→                        pid=proc_manager._process.pid,\n   588→                        poll_result=\"running\",\n   589→                        elapsed=round(_elapsed, 1),\n   590→                        output_bytes=ms.output_bytes,\n   591→                        growth_rate=round(ms.growth_rate_bps, 1),\n   592→                        stall_seconds=round(ms.stall_seconds, 1),\n   593→                        stall_status=ms.stall_status,\n   594→                    )\n   595→\n   596→                    # --- Watchdog: stall timeout check ---\n   597→                    if (\n   598→                        config.stall_timeout > 0\n   599→                        and ms.stall_seconds > config.stall_timeout\n   600→                        and ms.events_received > 0  # don't trigger during startup\n   601→                        and not _stall_acted\n   602→                    ):\n   603→                        _stall_acted = True\n   604→                        debug_log(\n   605→                            _dbg,\n   606→                            \"watchdog_triggered\",\n   607→                            phase=phase.number,\n   608→                            action=config.stall_action,\n   609→                            stall_seconds=round(ms.stall_seconds, 1),\n   610→                            pid=proc_manager._process.pid,\n   611→                        )\n   612→                        if config.stall_action == \"kill\":\n   613→                            import sys\n   614→                            print(\n   615→                                f\"[WATCHDOG] Stall detected ({ms.stall_seconds:.0f}s > \"\n   616→                                f\"{config.stall_timeout}s) — killing phase {phase.number}\",\n   617→                                file=sys.stderr,\n   618→                            )\n   619→                            _timed_out = True\n   620→                            proc_manager.terminate()\n   621→                            break\n   622→                        else:\n   623→                            # warn action: log and continue\n   624→                            import sys\n   625→                            print(\n   626→                                f\"[WATCHDOG] Stall detected ({ms.stall_seconds:.0f}s > \"\n   627→                                f\"{config.stall_timeout}s) — warning for phase {phase.number}\",\n   628→                                file=sys.stderr,\n   629→                            )\n   630→\n   631→                    # Reset single-fire guard when output resumes\n   632→                    if _stall_acted and ms.stall_seconds == 0.0:\n   633→                        _stall_acted = False\n   634→\n   635→                    # Update TUI at ~2 Hz (monitor thread handles data extraction)\n   636→                    # Wrap in try/except so a display glitch cannot abort the sprint\n   637→                    try:\n   638→                        tui.update(sprint_result, monitor.state, phase)\n   639→                    except Exception as _tui_exc:\n   640→                        import sys\n   641→                        print(f\"[TUI] Display error (continuing sprint): {_tui_exc}\", file=sys.stderr)\n   642→                    time.sleep(0.5)\n   643→\n   644→                # Safely read exit code: returncode may be None if terminate raced.\n   645→                # Use _timed_out flag instead of assigning directly to returncode.\n   646→                raw_rc = proc_manager._process.returncode\n   647→                if _timed_out:\n   648→                    exit_code = 124\n   649→                else:\n   650→                    exit_code = raw_rc if raw_rc is not None else -1\n   651→                monitor.stop()\n   652→                finished_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n   653→                _phase_dur = (finished_at - started_at).total_seconds()\n   654→                debug_log(\n   655→                    _dbg,\n   656→                    \"PHASE_END\",\n   657→                    phase=phase.number,\n   658→                    exit_code=exit_code,\n   659→                    duration=round(_phase_dur, 1),\n   660→                )\n   661→\n   662→                # If shutdown was requested during the poll loop, classify as\n   663→                # INTERRUPTED rather than letting _determine_phase_status see\n   664→                # exit_code=-1 (None→-1 fallback) and return PhaseStatus.ERROR,\n   665→                # which would incorrectly set the outcome to HALTED.\n   666→                if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n   667→                    logger.write_phase_interrupt(phase, started_at, finished_at, exit_code)\n   668→                    sprint_result.outcome = SprintOutcome.INTERRUPTED\n   669→                    break\n   670→\n   671→                # Determine phase status\n   672→                status = _determine_phase_status(\n   673→                    exit_code=exit_code,\n   674→                    result_file=config.result_file(phase),\n   675→                    output_file=config.output_file(phase),\n   676→                    config=config,\n   677→                    phase=phase,\n   678→                    started_at=started_at.timestamp(),\n   679→                    error_file=config.error_file(phase),\n   680→                )\n   681→\n   682→                # Write executor result file for downstream consumers.\n   683→                # Written AFTER status determination to avoid circularity.\n   684→                # Overwrites any agent-written file — executor is authoritative.\n   685→                _write_executor_result_file(\n   686→                    config=config,\n   687→                    phase=phase,\n   688→                    status=status,\n   689→                    exit_code=exit_code,\n   690→                    monitor_state=monitor.state,\n   691→                    started_at=started_at,\n   692→                    finished_at=finished_at,\n   693→                )\n   694→\n   695→                # Collect stderr size for telemetry\n   696→                error_file = config.error_file(phase)\n   697→                error_bytes = error_file.stat().st_size if error_file.exists() else 0\n   698→\n   699→                phase_result = PhaseResult(\n   700→                    phase=phase,\n   701→                    status=status,\n   702→                    exit_code=exit_code,\n   703→                    started_at=started_at,\n   704→                    finished_at=finished_at,\n   705→                    output_bytes=monitor.state.output_bytes,\n   706→                    error_bytes=error_bytes,\n   707→                    last_task_id=monitor.state.last_task_id,\n   708→                    files_changed=monitor.state.files_changed,\n   709→                )\n   710→                sprint_result.phase_results.append(phase_result)\n   711→\n   712→                debug_log(\n   713→                    _dbg,\n   714→                    \"phase_complete\",\n   715→                    phase=phase.number,\n   716→                    status=status.value,\n   717→                    exit_code=exit_code,\n   718→                    duration=round(_phase_dur, 1),\n   719→                )\n   720→\n   721→                # Log and notify\n   722→                logger.write_phase_result(phase_result)\n   723→                notify_phase_complete(phase_result)\n   724→\n   725→                tui.update(sprint_result, monitor.state, None)\n   726→\n   727→                # Decide: continue or halt?\n   728→                if status.is_failure:\n   729→                    # Collect diagnostics for the failed phase\n   730→                    try:\n   731→                        collector = DiagnosticCollector(config)\n   732→                        bundle = collector.collect(phase, phase_result, monitor.state)\n   733→                        classifier = FailureClassifier()\n   734→                        bundle.category = classifier.classify(bundle)\n   735→                        reporter = ReportGenerator()\n   736→                        diag_path = config.results_dir / f\"phase-{phase.number}-diagnostic.md\"\n   737→                        reporter.write(bundle, diag_path)\n   738→                        debug_log(\n   739→                            _dbg,\n   740→                            \"diagnostic_report\",\n   741→                            phase=phase.number,\n   742→                            category=bundle.category.value,\n   743→                            path=str(diag_path),\n   744→                        )\n   745→                    except Exception as _diag_exc:\n   746→                        debug_log(_dbg, \"diagnostic_error\", phase=phase.number, error=str(_diag_exc))\n   747→\n   748→                    sprint_result.outcome = SprintOutcome.HALTED\n   749→                    sprint_result.halt_phase = phase.number\n   750→                    break\n   751→\n   752→            finally:\n   753→                shutil.rmtree(isolation_dir, ignore_errors=True)\n   754→\n   755→        # Sprint finished\n   756→        sprint_result.finished_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n   757→        if sprint_result.outcome == SprintOutcome.SUCCESS:\n   758→            # Verify all phases actually passed\n   759→            if not all(r.status.is_success for r in sprint_result.phase_results):\n   760→                sprint_result.outcome = SprintOutcome.ERROR\n   761→\n   762→        tui.update(sprint_result, MonitorState(), None)\n   763→        logger.write_summary(sprint_result)\n   764→        notify_sprint_complete(sprint_result)\n   765→\n   766→    finally:\n   767→        # = sum(\n        1 for r in task_results if r.status == TaskStatus.PASS\n    )\n    report.tasks_failed = sum(\n        1 for r in task_results if r.status == TaskStatus.FAIL\n    )\n    report.tasks_incomplete = sum(\n        1 for r in task_results if r.status == TaskStatus.INCOMPLETE\n    )\n    report.tasks_skipped = sum(\n        1 for r in task_results if r.status == TaskStatus.SKIPPED\n    )\n    report.tasks_not_attempted = len(report.remaining_task_ids)\n    report.total_turns_consumed = sum(r.turns_consumed for r in task_results)\n    report.total_duration_seconds = sum(\n        r.duration_seconds for r in task_results\n    )\n\n    return report\n\n\ndef check_budget_guard(ledger: TurnLedger | None) -> str | None:\n    \"\"\"Pre-launch budget guard: returns a halt message if budget is insufficient.\n\n    Returns None if launch is allowed, or a descriptive message string\n    if the budget is too low to launch a subprocess.\n    \"\"\"\n    if ledger is None:\n        return None\n    if ledger.can_launch():\n        return None\n    return (\n        f\"Budget exhausted: {ledger.available()} turns remaining, \"\n        f\"minimum {ledger.minimum_allocation} required for launch\"\n    )\n\n\ndef execute_phase_tasks(\n    tasks: list[TaskEntry],\n    config: SprintConfig,\n    phase,\n    ledger: TurnLedger | None = None,\n    *,\n    _subprocess_factory=None,\n) -> tuple[list[TaskResult], list[str]]:\n    \"\"\"Per-task subprocess orchestration loop.\n\n    Iterates over a task inventory, spawning one subprocess per task with\n    budget allocation from the TurnLedger. Returns task results and a list\n    of remaining (unattempted) task IDs if budget was exhausted.\n\n    Args:\n        tasks: Ordered list of TaskEntry from the tasklist parser.\n        config: Sprint configuration.\n        phase: The Phase being executed.\n        ledger: Optional TurnLedger for budget tracking.\n        _subprocess_factory: Optional callable for testing; signature\n            ``(task, config, phase) -> (exit_code, turns_consumed, output_bytes)``.\n\n    Returns:\n        Tuple of (results, remaining_task_ids). remaining_task_ids is non-empty\n        only when the loop halted due to budget exhaustion.\n    \"\"\"\n    results: list[TaskResult] = []\n    remaining: list[str] = []\n\n    if not tasks:\n        return results, remaining\n\n    for i, task in enumerate(tasks):\n        started_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n\n        # Budget check: can we launch?\n        if ledger is not None and not ledger.can_launch():\n            # Mark this and all subsequent tasks as skipped\n            remaining = [t.task_id for t in tasks[i:]]\n            for t in tasks[i:]:\n                results.append(\n                    TaskResult(\n                        task=t,\n                        status=TaskStatus.SKIPPED,\n                        started_at=started_at,\n                        finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n                    )\n                )\n            break\n\n        # Debit the minimum allocation upfront\n        if ledger is not None:\n            ledger.debit(ledger.minimum_allocation)\n\n        # Spawn subprocess for this task\n        if _subprocess_factory is not None:\n            exit_code, turns_consumed, output_bytes = _subprocess_factory(\n                task, config, phase\n            )\n        else:\n            # Default: delegate to ClaudeProcess (real execution)\n            exit_code, turns_consumed, output_bytes = _run_task_subprocess(\n                task, config, phase\n            )\n\n        finished_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n\n        # Determine task status from exit code\n        if exit_code == 0:\n            status = TaskStatus.PASS\n        elif exit_code == 124:\n            status = TaskStatus.INCOMPLETE\n        else:\n            status = TaskStatus.FAIL\n\n        # Reconcile budget: debit actual consumption, credit back pre-allocation\n        if ledger is not None:\n            # We pre-debited minimum_allocation; now adjust for actual turns\n            actual = max(turns_consumed, 0)\n            pre_allocated = ledger.minimum_allocation\n            if actual > pre_allocated:\n                ledger.debit(actual - pre_allocated)\n            elif actual < pre_allocated:\n                ledger.credit(pre_allocated - actual)\n\n        results.append(\n            TaskResult(\n                task=task,\n                status=status,\n                turns_consumed=turns_consumed,\n                exit_code=exit_code,\n                started_at=started_at,\n                finished_at=finished_at,\n                output_bytes=output_bytes,\n            )\n        )\n\n    return results, remaining\n\n\ndef _run_task_subprocess(\n    task: TaskEntry,\n    config: SprintConfig,\n    phase,\n) -> tuple[int, int, int]:\n    \"\"\"Run a single task in a subprocess. Returns (exit_code, turns, output_bytes).\n\n    This is the real implementation that spawns a ClaudeProcess. For testing,\n    callers of execute_phase_tasks pass _subprocess_factory instead.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Build a task-specific prompt\n    prompt = (\n        f\"Execute task {task.task_id}: {task.title}\\n\"\n        f\"From phase file: {phase.file}\\n\"\n        f\"Description: {task.description}\\n\"\n    )\n\n    proc = ClaudeProcess.__new__(ClaudeProcess)\n    proc.config = config\n    proc.phase = phase\n    from superclaude.cli.pipeline.process import ClaudeProcess as _Base\n    _Base.__init__(\n        proc,\n        prompt=prompt,\n        output_file=config.output_file(phase),\n        error_file=config.error_file(phase),\n        max_turns=config.max_turns,\n        model=config.model,\n        permission_flag=config.permission_flag,\n        timeout_seconds=config.max_turns * 120 + 300,\n        output_format=\"stream-json\",\n    )\n    proc.start()\n    proc.wait()\n    exit_code = proc._process.returncode if proc._process else -1\n    output_path = config.output_file(phase)\n    output_bytes = output_path.stat().st_size if output_path.exists() else 0\n    # Turn counting is wired separately in T02.06\n    return (exit_code if exit_code is not None else -1, 0, output_bytes)\n\n\ndef execute_sprint(config: SprintConfig):\n    \"\"\"Main orchestration loop.\n\n    For each active phase:\n    1. Launch claude -p subprocess\n    2. Start output monitor thread\n    3. Update TUI in a polling loop until process exits (with timeout)\n    4. Parse result file for CONTINUE/HALT\n    5. Record PhaseResult\n    6. Decide whether to continue or halt\n    \"\"\"\n    # Pre-flight: verify claude binary is available before starting TUI/logging\n    if shutil.which(\"claude\") is None:\n        raise SystemExit(\n            \"Error: 'claude' binary not found in PATH. \"\n            \"Install Claude Code CLI before running sprint.\"\n        )\n\n    signal_handler = SignalHandler()\n    signal_handler.install()\n\n    setup_debug_logger(config)\n    import logging as _logging\n    _dbg = _logging.getLogger(_DBG_NAME)\n\n    logger = SprintLogger(config)\n    tui = SprintTUI(config)\n    monitor = OutputMonitor(Path(\"/dev/null\"))  # reset per phase\n    proc_manager: ClaudeProcess | None = None\n\n    sprint_result = SprintResult(config=config)\n    logger.write_header(sprint_result)\n\n    tui.start()\n\n    # Startup orphan cleanup: remove stale isolation dirs from crashed previous runs\n    shutil.rmtree(config.results_dir / \".isolation\", ignore_errors=True)\n\n    try:\n        for phase in config.active_phases:\n            if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n                sprint_result.outcome = SprintOutcome.INTERRUPTED\n                break\n\n            # Per-phase isolation directory: exactly one file (the phase file)\n            isolation_dir = config.results_dir / \".isolation\" / f\"phase-{phase.number}\"\n            isolation_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n            shutil.copy2(phase.file, isolation_dir / phase.file.name)\n\n            try:\n                # Reset monitor for this phase\n                output_path = config.output_file(phase)\n                monitor.reset(output_path)\n                monitor.start()\n\n                # Update tmux tail pane if running in tmux\n                if config.tmux_session_name:\n                    update_tail_pane(config.tmux_session_name, output_path)\n\n                # Launch claude with isolation env vars (CLAUDE_WORK_DIR → isolation_dir)\n                _phase_env_vars = {\n                    \"CLAUDE_WORK_DIR\": str(isolation_dir),\n                }\n                proc_manager = ClaudeProcess(config, phase, env_vars=_phase_env_vars)\n                proc_manager.start()\n                started_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n                # Use monotonic clock for deadline enforcement to be immune to NTP adjustments\n                deadline = time.monotonic() + proc_manager.timeout_seconds\n                logger.write_phase_start(phase, started_at)\n\n                debug_log(_dbg, \"PHASE_BEGIN\", phase=phase.number, file=str(phase.file))\n\n                tui.update(sprint_result, monitor.state, phase)\n\n                # Poll loop: wait for process to finish while updating TUI\n                # Enforces monotonic timeout via deadline check.\n                _timed_out = False\n                _stall_acted = False  # single-fire guard for watchdog\n                _poll_start = time.monotonic()\n                while proc_manager._process.poll() is None:\n                    if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n                        proc_manager.terminate()\n                        break\n                    if time.monotonic() > deadline:\n                        # Timeout reached: kill the process, exit loop\n                        _timed_out = True\n                        proc_manager.terminate()\n                        break\n\n                    ms = monitor.state\n                    _elapsed = time.monotonic() - _poll_start\n\n                    debug_log(\n                        _dbg,\n                        \"poll_tick\",\n                        phase=phase.number,\n                        pid=proc_manager._process.pid,\n                        poll_result=\"running\",\n                        elapsed=round(_elapsed, 1),\n                        output_bytes=ms.output_bytes,\n                        growth_rate=round(ms.growth_rate_bps, 1),\n                        stall_seconds=round(ms.stall_seconds, 1),\n                        stall_status=ms.stall_status,\n                    )\n\n                    # --- Watchdog: stall timeout check ---\n                    if (\n                        config.stall_timeout > 0\n                        and ms.stall_seconds > config.stall_timeout\n                        and ms.events_received > 0  # don't trigger during startup\n                        and not _stall_acted\n                    ):\n                        _stall_acted = True\n                        debug_log(\n                            _dbg,\n                            \"watchdog_triggered\",\n                            phase=phase.number,\n                            action=config.stall_action,\n                            stall_seconds=round(ms.stall_seconds, 1),\n                            pid=proc_manager._process.pid,\n                        )\n                        if config.stall_action == \"kill\":\n                            import sys\n                            print(\n                                f\"[WATCHDOG] Stall detected ({ms.stall_seconds:.0f}s > \"\n                                f\"{config.stall_timeout}s) — killing phase {phase.number}\",\n                                file=sys.stderr,\n                            )\n                            _timed_out = True\n                            proc_manager.terminate()\n                            break\n                        else:\n                            # warn action: log and continue\n                            import sys\n                            print(\n                                f\"[WATCHDOG] Stall detected ({ms.stall_seconds:.0f}s > \"\n                                f\"{config.stall_timeout}s) — warning for phase {phase.number}\",\n                                file=sys.stderr,\n                            )\n\n                    # Reset single-fire guard when output resumes\n                    if _stall_acted and ms.stall_seconds == 0.0:\n                        _stall_acted = False\n\n                    # Update TUI at ~2 Hz (monitor thread handles data extraction)\n                    # Wrap in try/except so a display glitch cannot abort the sprint\n                    try:\n                        tui.update(sprint_result, monitor.state, phase)\n                    except Exception as _tui_exc:\n                        import sys\n                        print(f\"[TUI] Display error (continuing sprint): {_tui_exc}\", file=sys.stderr)\n                    time.sleep(0.5)\n\n                # Safely read exit code: returncode may be None if terminate raced.\n                # Use _timed_out flag instead of assigning directly to returncode.\n                raw_rc = proc_manager._process.returncode\n                if _timed_out:\n                    exit_code = 124\n                else:\n                    exit_code = raw_rc if raw_rc is not None else -1\n                monitor.stop()\n                finished_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n                _phase_dur = (finished_at - started_at).total_seconds()\n                debug_log(\n                    _dbg,\n                    \"PHASE_END\",\n                    phase=phase.number,\n                    exit_code=exit_code,\n                    duration=round(_phase_dur, 1),\n                )\n\n                # If shutdown was requested during the poll loop, classify as\n                # INTERRUPTED rather than letting _determine_phase_status see\n                # exit_code=-1 (None→-1 fallback) and return PhaseStatus.ERROR,\n                # which would incorrectly set the outcome to HALTED.\n                if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n                    logger.write_phase_interrupt(phase, started_at, finished_at, exit_code)\n                    sprint_result.outcome = SprintOutcome.INTERRUPTED\n                    break\n\n                # Determine phase status\n                status = _determine_phase_status(\n                    exit_code=exit_code,\n                    result_file=config.result_file(phase),\n                    output_file=config.output_file(phase),\n                    config=config,\n                    phase=phase,\n                    started_at=started_at.timestamp(),\n                    error_file=config.error_file(phase),\n                )\n\n                # Write executor result file for downstream consumers.\n                # Written AFTER status determination to avoid circularity.\n                # Overwrites any agent-written file — executor is authoritative.\n                _write_executor_result_file(\n                    config=config,\n                    phase=phase,\n                    status=status,\n                    exit_code=exit_code,\n                    monitor_state=monitor.state,\n                    started_at=started_at,\n                    finished_at=finished_at,\n                )\n\n                # Collect stderr size for telemetry\n                error_file = config.error_file(phase)\n                error_bytes = error_file.stat().st_size if error_file.exists() else 0\n\n                phase_result = PhaseResult(\n                    phase=phase,\n                    status=status,\n                    exit_code=exit_code,\n                    started_at=started_at,\n                    finished_at=finished_at,\n                    output_bytes=monitor.state.output_bytes,\n                    error_bytes=error_bytes,\n                    last_task_id=monitor.state.last_task_id,\n                    files_changed=monitor.state.files_changed,\n                )\n                sprint_result.phase_results.append(phase_result)\n\n                debug_log(\n                    _dbg,\n                    \"phase_complete\",\n                    phase=phase.number,\n                    status=status.value,\n                    exit_code=exit_code,\n                    duration=round(_phase_dur, 1),\n                )\n\n                # Log and notify\n                logger.write_phase_result(phase_result)\n                notify_phase_complete(phase_result)\n\n                tui.update(sprint_result, monitor.state, None)\n\n                # Decide: continue or halt?\n                if status.is_failure:\n                    # Collect diagnostics for the failed phase\n                    try:\n                        collector = DiagnosticCollector(config)\n                        bundle = collector.collect(phase, phase_result, monitor.state)\n                        classifier = FailureClassifier()\n                        bundle.category = classifier.classify(bundle)\n                        reporter = ReportGenerator()\n                        diag_path = config.results_dir / f\"phase-{phase.number}-diagnostic.md\"\n                        reporter.write(bundle, diag_path)\n                        debug_log(\n                            _dbg,\n                            \"diagnostic_report\",\n                            phase=phase.number,\n                            category=bundle.category.value,\n                            path=str(diag_path),\n                        )\n                    except Exception as _diag_exc:\n                        debug_log(_dbg, \"diagnostic_error\", phase=phase.number, error=str(_diag_exc))\n\n                    sprint_result.outcome = SprintOutcome.HALTED\n                    sprint_result.halt_phase = phase.number\n                    break\n\n            finally:\n                shutil.rmtree(isolation_dir, ignore_errors=True)\n\n        # Sprint finished\n        sprint_result.finished_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n        if sprint_result.outcome == SprintOutcome.SUCCESS:\n            # Verify all phases actually passed\n            if not all(r.status.is_success for r in sprint_result.phase_results):\n                sprint_result.outcome = SprintOutcome.ERROR\n\n        tui.update(sprint_result, MonitorState(), None)\n        logger.write_summary(sprint_result)\n        notify_sprint_complete(sprint_result)\n\n    finally:\n        # Ensure monitor thread and subprocess are cleaned up even on exception.\n        # Each step is independent so one failure does not prevent others.\n        try:\n            monitor.stop()\n        except Exception:\n            pass\n        if proc_manager is not None:\n            try:\n                proc_manager.terminate()\n            except Exception:\n                pass\n        try:\n            tui.stop()\n        except Exception:\n            pass\n        try:\n            signal_handler.uninstall()\n        except Exception:\n            pass\n\n    # Write sentinel exit code file so tmux caller can read the outcome\n    _exitcode = 0 if sprint_result.outcome == SprintOutcome.SUCCESS else 1\n    try:\n        (config.release_dir / \".sprint-exitcode\").write_text(str(_exitcode))\n    except OSError:\n        pass  # best-effort; do not mask the real exit\n\n    if _exitcode != 0:\n        raise SystemExit(_exitcode)\n\n\ndef _classify_from_result_file(\n    result_file: Path,\n    started_at: float,\n) -> PhaseStatus | None:\n    \"\"\"Classify phase outcome from the agent-written result file.\n\n    Returns a PhaseStatus if the result file exists, is fresh (mtime > started_at),\n    and contains a recognizable EXIT_RECOMMENDATION. Returns None if the file is\n    missing, stale, or unreadable.\n    \"\"\"\n    if not result_file.exists():\n        return None\n    try:\n        mtime = result_file.stat().st_mtime\n    except OSError:\n        return None\n    if started_at > 0 and mtime < started_at:\n        # Stale file from a previous run — do not trust\n        return None\n    try:\n        content = result_file.read_text(errors=\"replace\")\n    except OSError:\n        return None\n    upper = content.upper()\n    if \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT\" in upper:\n        return PhaseStatus.HALT\n    if \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\" in upper:\n        return PhaseStatus.PASS_RECOVERED\n    if re.search(r\"status:\\s*PASS\\b\", content, re.IGNORECASE):\n        return PhaseStatus.PASS_RECOVERED\n    if re.search(r\"status:\\s*FAIL(?:ED|URE)?\\b\", content, re.IGNORECASE):\n        return PhaseStatus.HALT\n    if re.search(r\"status:\\s*PARTIAL\\b\", content, re.IGNORECASE):\n        return PhaseStatus.INCOMPLETE\n    return None\n\n\ndef _check_checkpoint_pass(config: SprintConfig, phase: Phase) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Return True if the end-of-phase checkpoint file exists with status PASS.\"\"\"\n    checkpoint_path = config.release_dir / \"checkpoints\" / f\"CP-P{phase.number:02d}-END.md\"\n    if not checkpoint_path.exists():\n        return False\n    try:\n        content = checkpoint_path.read_text(errors=\"replace\").upper()\n        return \"STATUS: PASS\" in content or \"**RESULT**: PASS\" in content\n    except OSError:\n        return False\n\n\ndef _check_contamination(config: SprintConfig, phase: Phase) -> list[str]:\n    \"\"\"Return list of artifact files containing cross-phase task ID patterns.\"\"\"\n    import re as _re\n\n    contaminated: list[str] = []\n    artifacts_dir = config.release_dir / \"artifacts\"\n    if not artifacts_dir.exists():\n        return contaminated\n    next_phase = phase.number + 1\n    pattern = _re.compile(rf\"T{next_phase:02d}\\.\\d{{2}}\", _re.IGNORECASE)\n    for md_file in artifacts_dir.rglob(\"*.md\"):\n        try:\n            if results/crash_recovery_log.md.\"\"\"\n    log_path = config.results_dir / \"crash_recovery_log.md\"\n    entry = (\n        f\"\\n## Phase {phase.number} — PASS_RECOVERED Recovery\\n\"\n        f\"**Timestamp**: {datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()}\\n\"\n        f\"**Checkpoint**: checkpoints/CP-P{phase.number:02d}-END.md (PASS)\\n\"\n        f\"**Contamination check**: \"\n        + try:\n        with open(log_path, \"a\") as f:\n            f.write(entry)\n    except OSError:\n        pass\n\n\ndef _write_executor_result_file(\n    config: SprintConfig,\n    phase: Phase,\n    status: PhaseStatus,\n    exit_code: int,\n    monitor_state: MonitorState,\n    started_at: datetime,\n    finished_at: datetime,\n) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Write executor-sourced result file for downstream consumers.\n\n    This is written AFTER _determine_phase_status returns, so it does not\n    create circularity. It provides a deterministic result file even when\n    the agent failed to write one.\n    \"\"\"\n    duration = (finished_at - started_at).total_seconds()\n    recommendation = \"CONTINUE\" if status.is_success else \"HALT\"\n    content = (\n        \"---\\n\"\n        f\"phase: {phase.number}\\n\"\n        f\"status: {'PASS' if status.is_success else 'FAIL'}\\n\"\n        f\"tasks_total: 1\\n\"\n        f\"tasks_passed: {1 if status.is_success else 0}\\n\"\n        f\"tasks_failed: {0 if status.is_success else 1}\\n\"\n        \"---\\n\"\n        \"\\n\"\n        f\"# Phase {phase.number} — Executor Result Report\\n\"\n        \"\\n\"\n        f\"| Phase | Status | Exit Code | Duration |\\n\"\n        f\"|-------|--------|-----------|----------|\\n\"\n        f\"| {phase.number} | {status.value} | {exit_code} | {duration:.1f}s |\\n\"\n        \"\\n\"\n        f\"**Source**: executor (not agent self-report)\\n\"\n        f\"**Output bytes**: {monitor_state.output_bytes}\\n\"\n        f\"**Last task ID**: {monitor_state.last_task_id or 'n/a'}\\n\"\n        f\"**Files changed**: {monitor_state.files_changed}\\n\"\n        \"\\n\"\n        f\"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: {recommendation}\\n\"\n    )\n    result_path = config.result_file(phase)\n    try:\n        result_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n        result_path.write_text(content)\n    except OSError:\n        pass  # Non-fatal — best effort\n\n\ndef _determine_phase_status(\n    exit_code: int,\n    result_file: Path,\n    output_file: Path,\n    *,\n    config: SprintConfig | None = None,\n    phase: Phase | None = None,\n    started_at: float = 0.0,\n    error_file: Path | None = None,\n) -> PhaseStatus:\n    \"\"\"Parse result file and exit code to determine phase status.\n\n    Priority:\n    1. Timeout (exit 124) -> TIMEOUT\n    2. Non-zero exit -> ERROR\n    3. Result file with EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT -> HALT\n    4. Result file with EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE -> PASS\n    5. Result file with status: PASS/FAIL -> PASS/HALT\n    6. No result file but output exists -> PASS_NO_REPORT\n    7. No result file and no output -> ERROR\n    \"\"\"\n    if exit_code == 124:\n        return PhaseStatus.TIMEOUT\n    if exit_code != 0:\n        # Path 1 — Specific: context exhaustion (Spec B S2)\n        # detect_prompt_too_long reads NDJSON output for \"Prompt is too long\"\n        if detect_prompt_too_long(output_file, error_path=error_file):\n            # Check if the agent managed to write a result file before exhaustion\n            result_status = _classify_from_result_file(result_file, started_at)\n            if result_status is not None:\n                return result_status\n            # No valid result file — context exhausted without completing\n            return PhaseStatus.INCOMPLETE\n\n        # Path 2 — General: checkpoint inference (Spec A SOL-C)\n        # Reads agent-written checkpoint files (pre-crash evidence)\n        if config is not None and phase is not None:\n            if _check_checkpoint_pass(config, phase):\n                contaminated = _check_contamination(config, phase)\n                _write_crash_recovery_log(config, phase, contaminated)\n                if not contaminated:\n                    return PhaseStatus.PASS_RECOVERED\n\n        # Path 3 — Default: unchanged\n        return PhaseStatus.ERROR\n\n    if result_file.exists():\n        content = result_file.read_text(errors=\"replace\")\n        # Use case-insensitive search for EXIT_RECOMMENDATION tokens to handle\n        # model output that varies in casing. When both CONTINUE and HALT appear\n        # (conflicting signals), HALT wins — the stronger/safer outcome.\n        upper = content.upper()\n        has_continue = \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\" in upper\n        has_halt = \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT\" in upper\n        if has_halt:\n            return PhaseStatus.HALT\n        if has_continue:\n            return PhaseStatus.PASS\n        if re.search(r\"status:\\s*PASS\\b\", content, re.IGNORECASE):\n            return PhaseStatus.PASS\n        if re.search(r\"status:\\s*FAIL(?:ED|URE)?\\b\", content, re.IGNORECASE):\n            return PhaseStatus.HALT\n        # PARTIAL result means tasks did not fully complete — treat as halt\n        if re.search(r\"status:\\s*PARTIAL\\b\", content, re.IGNORECASE):\n            return PhaseStatus.HALT\n        return PhaseStatus.PASS_NO_SIGNAL\n\n    if output_file.exists() and output_file.stat().st_size > 0:\n        # Check for budget exhaustion: a subprocess that exits 0 but hit\n        # error_max_turns produced no useful result — reclassify as INCOMPLETE\n        # to trigger HALT instead of silent continuation.\n        if detect_error_max_turns(output_file):\n            return PhaseStatus.INCOMPLETE\n        return PhaseStatus.PASS_NO_REPORT\n\n    return PhaseStatus.ERROR\n","numLines":1012,"startLine":1,"totalLines":1012}}}
